  <!-- JS -->
  <script src="https://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.4.1/jquery.min.js"></script>
  <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/intl-tel-input/17.0.8/js/intlTelInput.min.js"></script>

  <script>
  (function(){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
      var modal=document.getElementById('leadModal');
      var dialog=modal.querySelector('.onm-modal__dialog');
      var closeBtn=modal.querySelector('.onm-modal__close');

      let selectedPlano = null;

      function openModal(){ modal.classList.add('is-open'); document.body.style.overflow='hidden'; }
      function closeModal(){ modal.classList.remove('is-open'); document.body.style.overflow=''; }

      document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
        var opener=e.target.closest('.onm-sql'); 
        if(!opener) return;

        selectedPlano = opener.getAttribute('data-plano') || null;
        localStorage.setItem('onm_plano', selectedPlano || '197'); // salva para analytics
        document.cookie = 'onm_plano=' + (selectedPlano || '197') + '; path=/; domain=.onovomercado.com; Secure;';

        if(opener.tagName==='A') e.preventDefault(); 
        openModal();
      });

      modal.addEventListener('pointerdown',function(e){ if(!dialog.contains(e.target)) closeModal(); });
      dialog.addEventListener('pointerdown',function(e){ e.stopPropagation(); });
      closeBtn.addEventListener('click',closeModal);
      document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){ if(e.key==='Escape'&&modal.classList.contains('is-open')) closeModal(); });

      // intl-tel-input
      var phoneInput = document.getElementById('ac_phone');
      var iti;
      function initIti(){
        if(!window.intlTelInput || !phoneInput) return false;
        iti = window.intlTelInput(phoneInput, {
          initialCountry: 'br',
          separateDialCode: true,
          allowDropdown: true,
          preferredCountries: ['br','us'],
          utilsScript: 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/intl-tel-input/17.0.8/js/utils.js'
        });
        try{ iti.setCountry('br'); }catch(e){}
        return true;
      }
      if(!initIti()){ window.addEventListener('load', initIti); }

      phoneInput.addEventListener('keypress', function(e){
        if(!/[0-9]/.test(e.key)) e.preventDefault();
      });
      phoneInput.addEventListener('input', function(e){
        var isBR = (iti && iti.getSelectedCountryData().iso2 === 'br');
        var val = e.target.value || '';
        if(isBR){
          var dig = val.replace(/\D/g,'').match(/(\d{0,2})(\d{0,5})(\d{0,4})/);
          e.target.value = !dig[2] ? dig[1] : '('+dig[1]+') '+dig[2]+(dig[3] ? '-'+dig[3] : '');
        }else{
          e.target.value = val.replace(/\D/g,'');
        }
      });

      const form_list = '213';
      const form_tag = '304';
      const file_path = 'https://onovomercado.com/wp-content/themes/onovomercado/inc/ac-submit.php';

      const utm_pagina = '255', utm_source = '48', utm_campaign = '50', utm_medium = '49', utm_content = '52', utm_term = '51';

      const form = document.getElementById('acForm');
      const responseEl = document.getElementById('response');
      const nameInput = document.getElementById('ac_name');
      const emailInput = document.getElementById('ac_email');
      const btnSubmit = form.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
      const loaderEl = form.querySelector('.loader');
      const btnTxt = form.querySelector('.onm-btn-txt');

      function validarTelefone(fullE164, iso, dialCode){
        const digits = (fullE164||'').replace(/\D/g,'');
        if(!digits) return false;
        const after = digits.slice(String(dialCode||'55').length);
        return iso === 'br' ? /^[0-9]{10,11}$/.test(after) : after.length >= 6;
      }
      function validarEmail(email){ return /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]{2,}$/.test(email); }

      form.addEventListener('submit', function(event){
  event.preventDefault();

  const emailToValidate = emailInput.value;
  const phoneToValidate = iti ? iti.getNumber() : phoneInput.value;
  const countryData = iti ? iti.getSelectedCountryData() : { iso2:'br', dialCode:'55' };

  if (!validarEmail(emailToValidate)) {
    responseEl.innerText = 'Por favor, insira um e-mail válido.';
    return;
  }

  if (!validarTelefone(phoneToValidate, countryData.iso2, countryData.dialCode)) {
    responseEl.innerText = 'Telefone inválido.';
    return;
  }

  btnTxt.style.opacity = 0;
  loaderEl.style.display = 'block';
  btnSubmit.disabled = true;

  const form_name  = nameInput.value;
  const form_email = emailInput.value;
  const form_phone = phoneToValidate;

  try {
    localStorage.setItem('onm_name', form_name);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_email', form_email);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_phone', form_phone);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_utms', window.location.search);
  } catch(e) {}

  const cc_pg_cadastro = window.location.pathname.replace(/\//g,'') || 'home';
  const url_page = new URL(window.location.href);
  const params = url_page.searchParams;

  const cc_utm_source   = params.get('utm_source')   || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_medium   = params.get('utm_medium')   || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_campaign = params.get('utm_campaign') || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_term     = params.get('utm_term')     || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_content  = params.get('utm_content')  || 'organico';

  // Payload para ActiveCampaign
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    name: form_name,
    email: form_email,
    phone: form_phone,
    form_list: form_list,
    form_tag: form_tag,
    utm_data: [
      [utm_pagina, cc_pg_cadastro],
      [utm_source, cc_utm_source],
      [utm_campaign, cc_utm_campaign],
      [utm_medium, cc_utm_medium],
      [utm_content, cc_utm_content],
      [utm_term, cc_utm_term]
    ]
  });

  // Envio para ActiveCampaign
  try {
    if (navigator.sendBeacon) {
      const blob = new Blob([payload], { type: 'application/json' });
      navigator.sendBeacon(file_path, blob);
    } else {
      fetch(file_path, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: payload,
        keepalive: true
      });
    }
  } catch(e) {}

  // Redireciona para a página de planos (que vai montar a URL final com localStorage)
  setTimeout(function () {
    window.location.href = "https://onovomercado.com/escolha-seu-plano-home";
  }, 100);
});

    });
  })();
  </script>
</div>
				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
				</div>

<div class="w01-verificador-onm" id="verificador">
    <h2>Algum representante entrou em contato com você?</h2>
    <div class="w01-wrap">
        <form class="validador-form">
            <h3>Verifique nossos números oficiais:</h3>
            <input type="text" class="copy-phone" name="telefone" placeholder="(00) 00000-0000" maxlength="15" required="">
            <button type="submit">VERIFICAR</button>
        </form>
        <div class="copy-msg"></div>
    </div>

<script>
(function() {
    const numerosValidos = [
    '(13) 93300-9687',
    '(13) 92001-7494',
    '(11) 5116-8289',
    '(13) 4042-4626',
    '(13) 4042-4642',
    '(13) 99606-6485',
    '(13) 99671-0715',
    '(13) 99660-4893',
    '(13) 99746-8093',
    '(13) 99614-6910',
    '(13) 99619-4584',
    '(13) 99660-8684',
    '(13) 93300-0797',
    '(13) 99783-0270',
    '(31) 95347-5617',
    '(13) 92003-6189',
    '(13) 92003-6190',
    '(13) 92003-6187',
    '(13) 92003-6188',
    '(13) 92003-6069',
    '(13) 92003-6068',
    '(13) 92003-6064',
    '(13) 92003-6065',
    '(11) 91720-2850',
    '(13) 99183-1615'
];


    function mtel(v) {
        v = v.replace(/\D/g, "");
        v = v.replace(/^(\d{2})(\d)/g, "($1) $2");
        v = v.replace(/(\d)(\d{4})$/, "$1-$2");
        return v;
    }

    document.querySelectorAll(".w01-verificador-onm .validador-form").forEach(form => {
        const input = form.querySelector(".copy-phone");
        const msg = form.closest(".w01-wrap").querySelector(".copy-msg");

        input.addEventListener("keyup", function () {
            this.value = mtel(this.value);
        });

        input.addEventListener("change", function () {
            this.value = mtel(this.value);
        });

        form.addEventListener("submit", function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const tel = input.value;
            const valid = numerosValidos.includes(tel);
            msg.innerHTML = valid
                ? `<p class="p01 green">O número ${tel} é um número oficial.</p>
                <p class="p02">Você pode confiar nesse número, ele faz parte da equipe.</p>`
                : `<p class="p01 red">O número ${tel} não é um número oficial.</p>
                <p class="p02">Esse número não faz parte da equipe. Por favor, entre em contato com nosso <a href="https://api.whatsapp.com/send?phone=5513996066485&text=Ol%C3%A1%2C+recebi+um+contato+nao+oficial" target="_blank">suporte</a>.</p>`;
        });

        const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        if (params.has("phone")) {
            input.value = mtel(params.get("phone"));
            form.dispatchEvent(new Event('submit'));
        }
    });
})();
</script>				</div>

  <!-- Modal + Form -->
  <div id="leadModal" class="onm-modal" aria-hidden="true">
    <div class="onm-modal__backdrop"></div>
    <div class="onm-modal__dialog" role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby="leadModalTitle">
      <div class="onm-modal__panel">
        <button type="button" class="onm-modal__close" aria-label="Fechar">×</button>

          <form id="acForm" class="form_sql" autocomplete="on">

              Preencha seus dados abaixo para saber mais:

              <div class="onm-btn-txt">Quero saber mais</div>

                Termos de Uso e Política de Privacidade

  <!-- JS -->
  <script src="https://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.4.1/jquery.min.js"></script>
  <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/intl-tel-input/17.0.8/js/intlTelInput.min.js"></script>

  <script>
  (function(){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
      var modal=document.getElementById('leadModal');
      var dialog=modal.querySelector('.onm-modal__dialog');
      var closeBtn=modal.querySelector('.onm-modal__close');

      let selectedPlano = null;

      function openModal(){ modal.classList.add('is-open'); document.body.style.overflow='hidden'; }
      function closeModal(){ modal.classList.remove('is-open'); document.body.style.overflow=''; }

      document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
        var opener=e.target.closest('.onm-sql'); 
        if(!opener) return;

        selectedPlano = opener.getAttribute('data-plano') || null;
        localStorage.setItem('onm_plano', selectedPlano || '197'); // salva para analytics
        document.cookie = 'onm_plano=' + (selectedPlano || '197') + '; path=/; domain=.onovomercado.com; Secure;';

        if(opener.tagName==='A') e.preventDefault(); 
        openModal();
      });

      modal.addEventListener('pointerdown',function(e){ if(!dialog.contains(e.target)) closeModal(); });
      dialog.addEventListener('pointerdown',function(e){ e.stopPropagation(); });
      closeBtn.addEventListener('click',closeModal);
      document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){ if(e.key==='Escape'&&modal.classList.contains('is-open')) closeModal(); });

      // intl-tel-input
      var phoneInput = document.getElementById('ac_phone');
      var iti;
      function initIti(){
        if(!window.intlTelInput || !phoneInput) return false;
        iti = window.intlTelInput(phoneInput, {
          initialCountry: 'br',
          separateDialCode: true,
          allowDropdown: true,
          preferredCountries: ['br','us'],
          utilsScript: 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/intl-tel-input/17.0.8/js/utils.js'
        });
        try{ iti.setCountry('br'); }catch(e){}
        return true;
      }
      if(!initIti()){ window.addEventListener('load', initIti); }

      phoneInput.addEventListener('keypress', function(e){
        if(!/[0-9]/.test(e.key)) e.preventDefault();
      });
      phoneInput.addEventListener('input', function(e){
        var isBR = (iti && iti.getSelectedCountryData().iso2 === 'br');
        var val = e.target.value || '';
        if(isBR){
          var dig = val.replace(/\D/g,'').match(/(\d{0,2})(\d{0,5})(\d{0,4})/);
          e.target.value = !dig[2] ? dig[1] : '('+dig[1]+') '+dig[2]+(dig[3] ? '-'+dig[3] : '');
        }else{
          e.target.value = val.replace(/\D/g,'');
        }
      });

      const form_list = '213';
      const form_tag = '304';
      const file_path = 'https://onovomercado.com/wp-content/themes/onovomercado/inc/ac-submit.php';

      const utm_pagina = '255', utm_source = '48', utm_campaign = '50', utm_medium = '49', utm_content = '52', utm_term = '51';

      const form = document.getElementById('acForm');
      const responseEl = document.getElementById('response');
      const nameInput = document.getElementById('ac_name');
      const emailInput = document.getElementById('ac_email');
      const btnSubmit = form.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
      const loaderEl = form.querySelector('.loader');
      const btnTxt = form.querySelector('.onm-btn-txt');

      function validarTelefone(fullE164, iso, dialCode){
        const digits = (fullE164||'').replace(/\D/g,'');
        if(!digits) return false;
        const after = digits.slice(String(dialCode||'55').length);
        return iso === 'br' ? /^[0-9]{10,11}$/.test(after) : after.length >= 6;
      }
      function validarEmail(email){ return /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]{2,}$/.test(email); }

      form.addEventListener('submit', function(event){
  event.preventDefault();

  const emailToValidate = emailInput.value;
  const phoneToValidate = iti ? iti.getNumber() : phoneInput.value;
  const countryData = iti ? iti.getSelectedCountryData() : { iso2:'br', dialCode:'55' };

  if (!validarEmail(emailToValidate)) {
    responseEl.innerText = 'Por favor, insira um e-mail válido.';
    return;
  }

  if (!validarTelefone(phoneToValidate, countryData.iso2, countryData.dialCode)) {
    responseEl.innerText = 'Telefone inválido.';
    return;
  }

  btnTxt.style.opacity = 0;
  loaderEl.style.display = 'block';
  btnSubmit.disabled = true;

  const form_name  = nameInput.value;
  const form_email = emailInput.value;
  const form_phone = phoneToValidate;

  try {
    localStorage.setItem('onm_name', form_name);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_email', form_email);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_phone', form_phone);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_utms', window.location.search);
  } catch(e) {}

  const cc_pg_cadastro = window.location.pathname.replace(/\//g,'') || 'home';
  const url_page = new URL(window.location.href);
  const params = url_page.searchParams;

  const cc_utm_source   = params.get('utm_source')   || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_medium   = params.get('utm_medium')   || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_campaign = params.get('utm_campaign') || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_term     = params.get('utm_term')     || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_content  = params.get('utm_content')  || 'organico';

  // Payload para ActiveCampaign
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    name: form_name,
    email: form_email,
    phone: form_phone,
    form_list: form_list,
    form_tag: form_tag,
    utm_data: [
      [utm_pagina, cc_pg_cadastro],
      [utm_source, cc_utm_source],
      [utm_campaign, cc_utm_campaign],
      [utm_medium, cc_utm_medium],
      [utm_content, cc_utm_content],
      [utm_term, cc_utm_term]
    ]
  });

  // Envio para ActiveCampaign
  try {
    if (navigator.sendBeacon) {
      const blob = new Blob([payload], { type: 'application/json' });
      navigator.sendBeacon(file_path, blob);
    } else {
      fetch(file_path, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: payload,
        keepalive: true
      });
    }
  } catch(e) {}

  // Redireciona para a página de planos (que vai montar a URL final com localStorage)
  setTimeout(function () {
    window.location.href = "https://onovomercado.com/escolha-seu-plano-home/";
  }, 100);
});

    });
  })();
  </script>
</div>
				</div>
				</div>

" target="_blank" class="icon-whatsapp" rel="noopener">
  <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512"><!--!Font Awesome Free 6.5.2 by @fontawesome - https://fontawesome.com License - https://fontawesome.com/license/free Copyright 2024 Fonticons, Inc.--><path d="M380.9 97.1C339 55.1 283.2 32 223.9 32c-122.4 0-222 99.6-222 222 0 39.1 10.2 77.3 29.6 111L0 480l117.7-30.9c32.4 17.7 68.9 27 106.1 27h.1c122.3 0 224.1-99.6 224.1-222 0-59.3-25.2-115-67.1-157zm-157 341.6c-33.2 0-65.7-8.9-94-25.7l-6.7-4-69.8 18.3L72 359.2l-4.4-7c-18.5-29.4-28.2-63.3-28.2-98.2 0-101.7 82.8-184.5 184.6-184.5 49.3 0 95.6 19.2 130.4 54.1 34.8 34.9 56.2 81.2 56.1 130.5 0 101.8-84.9 184.6-186.6 184.6zm101.2-138.2c-5.5-2.8-32.8-16.2-37.9-18-5.1-1.9-8.8-2.8-12.5 2.8-3.7 5.6-14.3 18-17.6 21.8-3.2 3.7-6.5 4.2-12 1.4-32.6-16.3-54-29.1-75.5-66-5.7-9.8 5.7-9.1 16.3-30.3 1.8-3.7 .9-6.9-.5-9.7-1.4-2.8-12.5-30.1-17.1-41.2-4.5-10.8-9.1-9.3-12.5-9.5-3.2-.2-6.9-.2-10.6-.2-3.7 0-9.7 1.4-14.8 6.9-5.1 5.6-19.4 19-19.4 46.3 0 27.3 19.9 53.7 22.6 57.4 2.8 3.7 39.1 59.7 94.8 83.8 35.2 15.2 49 16.5 66.6 13.9 10.7-1.6 32.8-13.4 37.4-26.4 4.6-13 4.6-24.1 3.2-26.4-1.3-2.5-5-3.9-10.5-6.6z"/></svg>
</a> 				</div>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">

  <style>
    :root{
      --card-bg:#fff; --text:#0f172a; --muted:#64748b; --line:#e2e8f0;
      --accent:#ff2a6d; --accent-2:#ff5aa0; --radius:14px;

    #onm-sql-modal-root .onm-modal{position:fixed;inset:0;display:none;z-index:99999}
    #onm-sql-modal-root .onm-modal.is-open{display:block}
    #onm-sql-modal-root .onm-modal__backdrop{position:absolute;inset:0;background:rgba(2,6,23,.55);backdrop-filter:blur(2px)}

  <script src="https://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/3.4.1/jquery.min.js"></script>
  <script src="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/intl-tel-input/17.0.8/js/intlTelInput.min.js"></script>

  <script>
  (function(){
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
      var modal=document.getElementById('leadModal');
      var dialog=modal.querySelector('.onm-modal__dialog');
      var closeBtn=modal.querySelector('.onm-modal__close');

      let selectedPlano = null;

      function openModal(){ modal.classList.add('is-open'); document.body.style.overflow='hidden'; }
      function closeModal(){ modal.classList.remove('is-open'); document.body.style.overflow=''; }

      document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
        var opener=e.target.closest('.onm-sql'); 
        if(!opener) return;

        selectedPlano = opener.getAttribute('data-plano') || null;
        localStorage.setItem('onm_plano', selectedPlano || '197'); // salva para analytics
        document.cookie = 'onm_plano=' + (selectedPlano || '197') + '; path=/; domain=.onovomercado.com; Secure;';

        if(opener.tagName==='A') e.preventDefault(); 
        openModal();
      });

      modal.addEventListener('pointerdown',function(e){ if(!dialog.contains(e.target)) closeModal(); });
      dialog.addEventListener('pointerdown',function(e){ e.stopPropagation(); });
      closeBtn.addEventListener('click',closeModal);
      document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){ if(e.key==='Escape'&&modal.classList.contains('is-open')) closeModal(); });

      // intl-tel-input
      var phoneInput = document.getElementById('ac_phone');
      var iti;
      function initIti(){
        if(!window.intlTelInput || !phoneInput) return false;
        iti = window.intlTelInput(phoneInput, {
          initialCountry: 'br',
          separateDialCode: true,
          allowDropdown: true,
          preferredCountries: ['br','us'],
          utilsScript: 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/intl-tel-input/17.0.8/js/utils.js'
        });
        try{ iti.setCountry('br'); }catch(e){}
        return true;
      }
      if(!initIti()){ window.addEventListener('load', initIti); }

      phoneInput.addEventListener('keypress', function(e){
        if(!/[0-9]/.test(e.key)) e.preventDefault();
      });
      phoneInput.addEventListener('input', function(e){
        var isBR = (iti && iti.getSelectedCountryData().iso2 === 'br');
        var val = e.target.value || '';
        if(isBR){
          var dig = val.replace(/\D/g,'').match(/(\d{0,2})(\d{0,5})(\d{0,4})/);
          e.target.value = !dig[2] ? dig[1] : '('+dig[1]+') '+dig[2]+(dig[3] ? '-'+dig[3] : '');
        }else{
          e.target.value = val.replace(/\D/g,'');
        }
      });

      const form_list = '213';
      const form_tag = '304';
      const file_path = 'https://onovomercado.com/wp-content/themes/onovomercado/inc/ac-submit.php';

      const utm_pagina = '255', utm_source = '48', utm_campaign = '50', utm_medium = '49', utm_content = '52', utm_term = '51';

      const form = document.getElementById('acForm');
      const responseEl = document.getElementById('response');
      const nameInput = document.getElementById('ac_name');
      const emailInput = document.getElementById('ac_email');
      const btnSubmit = form.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
      const loaderEl = form.querySelector('.loader');
      const btnTxt = form.querySelector('.onm-btn-txt');

      function validarTelefone(fullE164, iso, dialCode){
        const digits = (fullE164||'').replace(/\D/g,'');
        if(!digits) return false;
        const after = digits.slice(String(dialCode||'55').length);
        return iso === 'br' ? /^[0-9]{10,11}$/.test(after) : after.length >= 6;
      }
      function validarEmail(email){ return /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]{2,}$/.test(email); }

      form.addEventListener('submit', function(event){
  event.preventDefault();

  const emailToValidate = emailInput.value;
  const phoneToValidate = iti ? iti.getNumber() : phoneInput.value;
  const countryData = iti ? iti.getSelectedCountryData() : { iso2:'br', dialCode:'55' };

  if (!validarEmail(emailToValidate)) {
    responseEl.innerText = 'Por favor, insira um e-mail válido.';
    return;
  }

  if (!validarTelefone(phoneToValidate, countryData.iso2, countryData.dialCode)) {
    responseEl.innerText = 'Telefone inválido.';
    return;
  }

  btnTxt.style.opacity = 0;
  loaderEl.style.display = 'block';
  btnSubmit.disabled = true;

  const form_name  = nameInput.value;
  const form_email = emailInput.value;
  const form_phone = phoneToValidate;

  try {
    localStorage.setItem('onm_name', form_name);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_email', form_email);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_phone', form_phone);
    localStorage.setItem('onm_utms', window.location.search);
  } catch(e) {}

  const cc_pg_cadastro = window.location.pathname.replace(/\//g,'') || 'home';
  const url_page = new URL(window.location.href);
  const params = url_page.searchParams;

  const cc_utm_source   = params.get('utm_source')   || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_medium   = params.get('utm_medium')   || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_campaign = params.get('utm_campaign') || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_term     = params.get('utm_term')     || 'organico';
  const cc_utm_content  = params.get('utm_content')  || 'organico';

  // Payload para ActiveCampaign
  const payload = JSON.stringify({
    name: form_name,
    email: form_email,
    phone: form_phone,
    form_list: form_list,
    form_tag: form_tag,
    utm_data: [
      [utm_pagina, cc_pg_cadastro],
      [utm_source, cc_utm_source],
      [utm_campaign, cc_utm_campaign],
      [utm_medium, cc_utm_medium],
      [utm_content, cc_utm_content],
      [utm_term, cc_utm_term]
    ]
  });

  // Envio para ActiveCampaign
  try {
    if (navigator.sendBeacon) {
      const blob = new Blob([payload], { type: 'application/json' });
      navigator.sendBeacon(file_path, blob);
    } else {
      fetch(file_path, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: payload,
        keepalive: true
      });
    }
  } catch(e) {}

  // Redireciona para a página de planos (que vai montar a URL final com localStorage)
  setTimeout(function () {
    window.location.href = "https://onovomercado.com/escolha-seu-plano-home/";
  }, 100);
});

    });
  })();
  </script>
</div>
				</div>
				</div>
					</div>
				</div>
				</div>
		</main>

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {

						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {

								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
